\n76: ## Migrations\n77: \n78: As your use of Grafana evolves, you may need to create _schema migrations_ for one or more database tables.\n79: \n80: To see all the types of migrations you can add, refer to [migrations.go](/pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/migrations.go).\n81: \n82: Before you add a migration, make sure that you:\n83: \n84: - Never change a migration that has been committed and pushed to `main`.\n85: - Always add new migrations, to change or undo previous migrations.\n86: \n87: Add a migration using one of the following methods:\n88: \n89: - Add migrations in the `migrations` package.\n90: - Implement the `DatabaseMigrator` for the service.\n91: \n92: > **Important:** If there are previous migrations for a service, use that method. interface. Supporting components include ResourceMigration and MigrationRunner for executing migrations, a MigrationRegistry for tracking available migrations, and resource registration logic. The UnifiedStorageMigrationService orchestrates the overall process, with validators ensuring data integrity and table locking mechanisms preventing concurrent access issues. database migration framework is composed of multiple layers and components:\\n\\n## Core Migration Framework (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/)\\nThe foundation is the Migrator struct in migrator.go, which tracks and executes migrations sequentially. It maintains a migration_log table to record executed migrations and prevents re-execution. The framework uses the Migration interface (types.go) for migration definitions, with CodeMigration for programmatic migrations and raw SQL migrations.\\n\\n## SQL Dialect Abstraction\\nThe Dialect interface (dialect.go) abstracts database-specific SQL generation. Three implementations exist:\\n- MySQLDialect (mysql_dialect.go) for MySQL with specific quoting and truncation behavior\\n- PostgresDialect (postgres_dialect.go) for PostgreSQL with NULLS LAST ordering\\n- SQLiteDialect (sqlite_dialect.go) for SQLite in-memory and file databases\\n\\nEach dialect handles database-specific features like JSON operations, array functions, and collation.\\n\\n## Migration Registration and Execution\\nOSSMigrations (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/migrations.go) is the main provider that registers all OSS migrations through the AddMigration method. The migrations.go file orchestrates dozens of individual migration files (alert_mig.go, dashboard_mig.go, user_mig.go, etc.) that define schema changes for different Grafana services. Each migration file uses a function pattern (e.g., addAlertMigrations) to register its changes with the Migrator.\\n\\n## Unified Storage Migration Framework\\nFor the new unified storage system, pkg/storage/unified/migrations/ provides a higher-level migration abstraction:\\n- UnifiedMigrator interface (migrator.go) handles bulk data migration for resource types\\n- MigrationRunner (resource_migration.go) executes migrations per-organization\\n- MigrationRegistry (registry.go) organizes migrations by resource type\\n- UnifiedStorageMigrationServiceImpl (service.go) is the Wire-provided entry point that runs migrations at startup\\n- Table locking (table_locker.go) prevents concurrent updates to legacy tables during migration\\n\\n## Migration Version Tracking\\nThe migration_log table stores migration history with MigrationLog struct fields: Id, MigrationID, and SQL. The Migrator checks this table during startup to skip already-executed migrations, supporting idempotent re-runs.\\n\\n## Rollback Handling\\nRollback functionality is implemented in pkg/services/secrets/migrator/migrator.go with the RollBackSecrets function, allowing migration reversal. The generic migration framework supports rollback through the migration design principle of always adding new migrations rather than modifying existing ones.\\n\\n## Database Initialization Flow\\n1. Database engine initialization (pkg/storage/unified/sql/db/dbimpl/dbimpl.go)\\n2. Migration.Run function (pkg/services/authz/zanzana/store/migration/migrator.go) is called with database type and config\\n3. Creates Migrator instance and registers OSSMigrations\\n4. Executes migrations with locking support\\n5. For unified storage, MigrateResourceStore (pkg/storage/unified/sql/db/migrations/migrator.go) is called\\n6. SQLStore.Migrate method (pkg/services/sqlstore/sqlstore.go) coordinates the full migration flow\\n\\nThe framework supports three database backends (MySQL, PostgreSQL, SQLite) with dialect-specific SQL while maintaining a unified migration interface. The version tracking table and locking mechanisms ensure safe, concurrent-safe migration execution during Grafana startup.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":12,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2203,"cache_read_input_tokens":95492,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2203},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"73ea86bd-49e7-4dd1-8a01-2d36e4108ea3","uuid":"ec23d229-3521-4972-9c1b-02fd5d68e353"}

database migration framework is composed of multiple layers and components:\\n\\n## Core Migration Framework (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/)\\nThe foundation is the Migrator struct in migrator.go, which tracks and executes migrations sequentially. It maintains a migration_log table to record executed migrations and prevents re-execution. The framework uses the Migration interface (types.go) for migration definitions, with CodeMigration for programmatic migrations and raw SQL migrations.\\n\\n## SQL Dialect Abstraction\\nThe Dialect interface (dialect.go) abstracts database-specific SQL generation. Three implementations exist:\\n- MySQLDialect (mysql_dialect.go) for MySQL with specific quoting and truncation behavior\\n- PostgresDialect (postgres_dialect.go) for PostgreSQL with NULLS LAST ordering\\n- SQLiteDialect (sqlite_dialect.go) for SQLite in-memory and file databases\\n\\nEach dialect handles database-specific features like JSON operations, array functions, and collation.\\n\\n## Migration Registration and Execution\\nOSSMigrations (pkg/services/sqlstore/migrations/migrations.go) is the main provider that registers all OSS migrations through the AddMigration method. The migrations.go file orchestrates dozens of individual migration files (alert_mig.go, dashboard_mig.go, user_mig.go, etc.) that define schema changes for different Grafana services. Each migration file uses a function pattern (e.g., addAlertMigrations) to register its changes with the Migrator.\\n\\n## Unified Storage Migration Framework\\nFor the new unified storage system, pkg/storage/unified/migrations/ provides a higher-level migration abstraction:\\n- UnifiedMigrator interface (migrator.go) handles bulk data migration for resource types\\n- MigrationRunner (resource_migration.go) executes migrations per-organization\\n- MigrationRegistry (registry.go) organizes migrations by resource type\\n- UnifiedStorageMigrationServiceImpl (service.go) is the Wire-provided entry point that runs migrations at startup\\n- Table locking (table_locker.go) prevents concurrent updates to legacy tables during migration\\n\\n## Migration Version Tracking\\nThe migration_log table stores migration history with MigrationLog struct fields: Id, MigrationID, and SQL. The Migrator checks this table during startup to skip already-executed migrations, supporting idempotent re-runs.\\n\\n## Rollback Handling\\nRollback functionality is implemented in pkg/services/secrets/migrator/migrator.go with the RollBackSecrets function, allowing migration reversal. The generic migration framework supports rollback through the migration design principle of always adding new migrations rather than modifying existing ones.\\n\\n## Database Initialization Flow\\n1. Database engine initialization (pkg/storage/unified/sql/db/dbimpl/dbimpl.go)\\n2. Migration.Run function (pkg/services/authz/zanzana/store/migration/migrator.go) is called with database type and config\\n3. Creates Migrator instance and registers OSSMigrations\\n4. Executes migrations with locking support\\n5. For unified storage, MigrateResourceStore (pkg/storage/unified/sql/db/migrations/migrator.go) is called\\n6. SQLStore.Migrate method (pkg/services/sqlstore/sqlstore.go) coordinates the full migration flow\\n\\nThe framework supports three database backends (MySQL, PostgreSQL, SQLite) with dialect-specific SQL while maintaining a unified migration interface. The version tracking table and locking mechanisms ensure safe, concurrent-safe migration execution during Grafana startup.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
